  \KeywordTok{load}\NormalTok{(cache_filepath)}
\NormalTok{  loaded_from_cache<-}\OtherTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}
\NormalTok{\{}
\NormalTok{  time_points <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{readr}\OperatorTok{::}\KeywordTok{read_csv}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(dropbbox_dir,}\StringTok{"/SST_roi_by_time_point.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\OperatorTok{!}\NormalTok{loaded_from_cache)\{}
\NormalTok{  roi_cols <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(time_points)[}\KeywordTok{grepl}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"harvardoxford"}\NormalTok{,}\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(time_points))]}
\NormalTok{time_points}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{tr_roi_mean <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rowMeans}\NormalTok{(time_points[,roi_cols])}
\NormalTok{time_points<-}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{time_points }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(subid,wave) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{run_mean_across_rois =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(tr_roi_mean, }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{#now mean-center the ROIs}
\NormalTok{time_points_c<-time_points}
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (roi_col }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ roi_cols)\{}
\NormalTok{  time_points_c[,roi_col]<-time_points_c[,roi_col]}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{time_points_c}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{run_mean_across_rois}
\NormalTok{\}}


\NormalTok{roi_detect_pattern<-}\StringTok{"((?<=harvardoxford-.\{0,3\}cortical_prob_)(.*))|(CueFollowing}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{(CS}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{>FS}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{).*)"}

\NormalTok{roi_cols_vec <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(time_points_c) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{stringr}\OperatorTok{::}\KeywordTok{str_detect}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{pattern =}\NormalTok{ roi_detect_pattern)}
\NormalTok{new_roi_cols <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(time_points_c) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{stringr}\OperatorTok{::}\KeywordTok{str_extract_all}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{pattern =}\NormalTok{ roi_detect_pattern) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{unlist}
\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(new_roi_cols)}
\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(time_points_c)[roi_cols_vec] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{new_roi_cols}

\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

We need to group by subject, wave, and trial, select just the FailedStop
trials, and just the high trial numbers, then get the min and max
accumbens activity. We could even do a long transform across the ROIs,
then also group by ROI and get the min and max for ROIs

So let's first long transform the ROIs

Then do the grouping and summarizing.

We define a peak period and trough period based on the previously
observed shape of the accumbens response in the FS trial. This will put
a peak around 2-6 seconds and a trough around 7-10 seconds. These values
were chosen subjectively to try to encompass the peak and trough
allowing for as much variability as possible without grabbing unrelated
data from other time points. With a TR of 2.0 we should always have one
or two images to grab from within these ranges, too.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\OperatorTok{!}\NormalTok{loaded_from_cache)\{}
\NormalTok{  tpc_long<-time_points_c }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{pivot_longer}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{cols=}\KeywordTok{all_of}\NormalTok{(new_roi_cols),}\DataTypeTok{names_to=}\StringTok{"ROI"}\NormalTok{,}\DataTypeTok{values_to=}\StringTok{"value"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  trial_summary_data <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tpc_long }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\CommentTok{#filter(condition=="FailedStop") %>% }
\StringTok{    }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(subid,wave,trial_n,ROI, condition) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{    }\KeywordTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}
      \DataTypeTok{peak=}\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
      \DataTypeTok{trough =} \KeywordTok{min}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
      \DataTypeTok{peak_time =}\NormalTok{ offset[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{][value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{]}\OperatorTok{==}\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)],}
      \DataTypeTok{trough_time =}\NormalTok{ offset[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{][value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{]}\OperatorTok{==}\KeywordTok{min}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{11.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)],}
      \DataTypeTok{med_post_trial =} \KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{4.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{10.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
      \DataTypeTok{med_post_trial_1_5 =} \KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(value[offset}\OperatorTok{>=}\FloatTok{1.0} \OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{offset }\OperatorTok{<=}\FloatTok{5.0}\NormalTok{],}\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
      
      
\NormalTok{    )}
    
  
\NormalTok{  trial_summary_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{response_amplitude <-trial_summary_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{peak}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{trial_summary_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{trough}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

OK. So now, let's try to merge in that with post-pre RTs. Where do we
get those from?

\hypertarget{basic-striatal-cluster-mixed-effects-models}{%
\section{Basic Striatal cluster mixed effects
models}\label{basic-striatal-cluster-mixed-effects-models}}

\hypertarget{all-trial-types-with-p_stop}{%
\section{All trial types, with
P\_Stop}\label{all-trial-types-with-p_stop}}

I think if you're going to do P\_stop

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  P\_stop\_trial seems mostly irrelevant and P\_stop\_trial\_post is a
  more relevant measure; P\_stop\_trial\_change is more relevant still.
\item
  measuring P\_stop\_trial rather than P\_stop\_trial\_change doesn't
  make much sense, but
\item
  If you're only measuring FS, neither P\_stop\_trial\_post nor
  P\_stop\_trial\_change are necessarily going to measure what you think
  because the data is censored to just FS trials, which are
  \emph{always} going to move in a particular direction
\item
  so while measuring \texttt{P\_stop\_trial}, it's best to do a model
  with all kinds of trials
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{table-1-stop-conditions-with-condition}{%
\subsection{Table 1: stop conditions, with
condition}\label{table-1-stop-conditions-with-condition}}

Modeled in more detail in
\texttt{modeling\_t\_5\_10\_activity\_as\_learning.Rmd}.

\textit{Note:}  & \multicolumn{3}{r}{$^{*}$p$<$0.1; $^{**}$p$<$0.05; $^{***}$p$<$0.01} \\ 
\end{tabular} 
\end{table}

\hypertarget{get-the-delay-to-next-trial}{%
\section{get the delay to next
trial}\label{get-the-delay-to-next-trial}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{behavioral_data_w_tone_data <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{readr}\OperatorTok{::}\KeywordTok{read_csv}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(dropbbox_dir,}\StringTok{"/sst_behavioral_data_all_w_class_type_reveal_onset.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## New names:
## Rows: 285696 Columns: 30
## -- Column specification
## -------------------------------------------------------- Delimiter: "," chr
## (4): subid, go_no_go_condition_label, condition, health_condition_label dbl
## (25): ...1, trial_n, numchunks_reciprocal, go_no_go_condition, arrow_pr... dttm
## (1): rundatetime
## i Use `spec()` to retrieve the full column specification for this data. i
## Specify the column types or set `show_col_types = FALSE` to quiet this message.
## * `` -> `...1`
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# I want to know: what is the time delay from the tone sound to the PERIOD of the next trial?}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{#so I want to match each trial up with the _next_ trial}
\CommentTok{#grab the set of next trials-we want their onset and their duration}
\CommentTok{#then match that back onto n+1 of their prior trial}
\NormalTok{trial_df <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{behavioral_data_w_tone_data }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{filter}\NormalTok{(condition}\OperatorTok{!=}\StringTok{"Cue"}\NormalTok{) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(trial_n) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(subid,waveid,runid) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{next_trial_n =} \KeywordTok{lead}\NormalTok{(trial_n,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}


\NormalTok{next_trial_df <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{behavioral_data_w_tone_data }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{filter}\NormalTok{(condition}\OperatorTok{!=}\StringTok{"Cue"}\NormalTok{) }\OperatorTok{%>%}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(trial_n,condition,onset,trial_duration,subid,waveid,runid)}


\NormalTok{trials_with_next<-}\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  trial_df,next_trial_df,}
  \DataTypeTok{by.x =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"subid"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"waveid"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"runid"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"next_trial_n"}\NormalTok{),}
  \DataTypeTok{by.y=}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"subid"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"waveid"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"runid"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"trial_n"}\NormalTok{),}
  \DataTypeTok{suffixes =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"_next"}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

now, mark for each trial the start and end time point of the next trial,
and get measures of how long after each trial the next one appears

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{trial_end_next <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{onset_next}\OperatorTok{+}\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{trial_duration_next}
\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start<-trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{onset_next}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset}
\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_end<-trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{trial_end_next}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{next_trial_median <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"next_trial_start_median"}\NormalTok{ =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start),}
  \StringTok{"next_trial_end_median"}\NormalTok{ =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_end)}
\NormalTok{  )}

\NormalTok{quantiles <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\OperatorTok{:}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{)}\OperatorTok{/}\DecValTok{10}
\CommentTok{# next_trial_gradient <- data.frame(}
\CommentTok{#   "quantiles" = quantiles,}
\CommentTok{#   "next_trial_start" = quantile(trials_with_next$class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start,(1:10)/10),}
\CommentTok{#   "next_trial_end" = quantile(trials_with_next$class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_end,(1:10)/10)}
\CommentTok{#   )}

\NormalTok{gradient_range =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{seq}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{floor}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{min}\NormalTok{(trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start)),}\KeywordTok{ceiling}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_end)),}\FloatTok{0.1}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{in_range_by_gradient <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sapply}\NormalTok{(gradient_range,}\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(tp)\{}
\NormalTok{  time_point_is_after_start <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tp }\OperatorTok{>}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start}
\NormalTok{  time_point_is_before_end <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tp }\OperatorTok{<}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_end}
\NormalTok{  number_of_trials <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(trials_with_next}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{class_type_reveal_onset_to_next_trial_start) }
  \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(time_point_is_after_start }\OperatorTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{time_point_is_before_end)}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{number_of_trials)}
\NormalTok{\})}

\NormalTok{next_trial_gradient <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"tp"}\NormalTok{=gradient_range,}\StringTok{"pct_in_range"}\NormalTok{=in_range_by_gradient)}
\NormalTok{next_trial_gradient}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{hrf_tp<-next_trial_gradient}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{tp}\OperatorTok{+}\DecValTok{5}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{cs-fs}{%
\subsection{CS-FS}\label{cs-fs}}

Let's now try to contrast these time series to see what the CS-FS looks
like. This will be interesting because it's similar to the simple GLM
result I got earlier that set me down the path of trying to analyze
this.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{trial_tps_compare_conditions<-df_offset }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{pivot_wider}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{id_cols=}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(offset_start),}\DataTypeTok{names_from =} \StringTok{"condition"}\NormalTok{,}\DataTypeTok{values_from=}\StringTok{"CueFollowing.CS.FS.striatal_cluster_combined"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{trial_tps_compare_conditions}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CS_minus_FS<-trial_tps_compare_conditions}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CorrectStop}\OperatorTok{-}\NormalTok{trial_tps_compare_conditions}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{FailedStop}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\includegraphics{sst_paper_generation_files/figure-latex/unnamed-chunk-26-1.pdf}

OK, so from this graph it is very clear why, during the subsequent
trial, we're seeing positive striatum activity, and it is also clear
there is a large dip in the same area right after the tone.
